Under General Andrew Jackson, U.S. military forces invaded the area, scattering Seminole villages, burning their towns.\r\n\r\nAs a result, in 1819 Spain was forced to surrender its Florida territory under the terms of the Transcontinental Treaty. One meeting they had was under a flag of truce. Once the Seminole parlays came to the fort to meet, the soldiers imprisoned them and the next morning they marched them off to Tampa to be removed from Florida in freight ships to Oklahoma ( Indian Territory). To break the moral of the Seminoles, the government broke apart the women and the men into different freight ships. Leaving their loved ones and their land that they fought and died for. The painting shows the couple having their last moment before being split up. The Seminole man is still in shackles and the two ships shows the separation of the couple.\r\n\r\nThey were shipped off to New Orleans bay, loaded up onto steamboats and traveled north up the Mississippi river and walked west from the Mississippi river through Arkansas to Oklahoma. They marched women, elders and babies, burying their family members as they journeyed to Oklahoma through the cold winter with limited resources and the cheapest material bought from the government to survive the trip.
